## Idea

As we iterate identity type (i.e., consider the type of identifications between
two identifications), the identity types gain further structure.

Identity types of identity types are types of the form `p ＝ q`, where
`p q : x ＝ y` and `x y : A`. Using the homotopy interpretation of type theory,
elements of such a type are often called _2-paths_ and a twice iterated identity
type is often called a _type of 2-paths_.

Since 2-paths are just identifications, they have the usual operations and
coherences on paths/identifications. In the context of 2-paths, this famliar
concatination operation is called vertical concatination (see
`vertical-concat-Id²` below). However, 2-paths have novel operations and
coherences derived from the operations and coherences of the boundary 1-paths
(these are `p` and `q` in the example above). Since concatination of 1-paths is
a functor, it has an induced action on paths. We call this operation horizontal
concatination (see `horizontal-concat-Id²` below). It comes with the standard
coherences of an action on paths function, as well as coherences induced by
coherences on the boundary 1-paths.

## Properties

### The unit laws of concatenation induce homotopies

<a id="3104" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#2981" class="Function">horizontal-unit-square</a> <a id="3127" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#3127" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="3129" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3131" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3545" class="Function">right-unit</a>

<a id="left-unit-law-horizontal-concat-square"></a><a id="3143" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#3143" class="Function">left-unit-law-horizontal-concat-square</a> <a id="3182" class="Symbol">:</a>

        <a id="4366" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="4368" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3349" class="Function">assoc</a> <a id="4374" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4145" class="Bound">p-ttop</a> <a id="4381" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4152" class="Bound">p-tright</a> <a id="4390" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4161" class="Bound">p-bright</a><a id="4398" class="Symbol">))))</a>

### Unit laws for `assoc`

We give two treatments of the unit laws for the associator. One for computing
with the associator, and one for coherences between the unit laws.

#### Computing `assoc` at a reflexivity

<pre class="Agda"><a id="4630" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="4637" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4637" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="4641" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4642" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4642" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4644" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4646" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4651" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4653" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4654" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4654" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4658" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4661" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4642" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4662" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4664" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4665" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4665" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4667" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4667" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4669" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4669" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="4671" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4673" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4654" class="Bound">A</a><a id="4674" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="4678" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="4687" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4687" class="Function">left-unit-law-assoc</a> <a id="4707" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="4713" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4714" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4714" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="4716" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4718" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4665" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4720" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="4722" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4667" class="Bound">y</a><a id="4723" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4725" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4726" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4726" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="4728" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4730" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4667" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4732" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="4734" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4669" class="Bound">z</a><a id="4735" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4737" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="4743" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3349" class="Function">assoc</a> <a id="4749" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="4754" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4714" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="4756" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4726" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="4758" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="4760" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
  <a id="4767" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4687" class="Function">left-unit-law-assoc</a> <a id="4787" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4787" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="4789" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4789" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="4791" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4793" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

  <a id="4801" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4801" class="Function">middle-unit-law-assoc</a> <a id="4823" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="5058" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#4940" class="Function">right-unit-law-assoc</a> <a id="5079" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="5084" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="5089" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5091" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>
#### Unit laws for `assoc` and their coherence

We use a binary naming scheme for the (higher) unit laws of the associator. For
each 3-digit binary number except when all digits are `1`, there is a
corresponding unit law. A `0` reflects that the unit of the operator is present
in the corresponding position. More generally, there is for each `n`-digit
binary number (except all `1`s) a unit law for the `n`-ary coherence operator.

href="foundation.path-algebra.html#13420" class="Bound">v</a><a id="13441" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13443" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="13447" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#7495" class="Function">horizontal-concat-Id²</a> <a id="13469" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13470" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="13475" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13476" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="13478" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13480" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#13406" class="Bound">p</a><a id="13481" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="13484" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#13432" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="13486" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a>
  <a id="13490" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#7785" class="Function">identification-left-whisk</a> <a id="13516" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#13406" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13518" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#13432" class="Bound">γ</a>
<a id="13520" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#13330" class="Function">left-unit-law-horizontal-concat-Id²</a> <a id="13556" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13558" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-binary-functions.html#2196" class="Function">left-unit-ap-binary</a> <a id="13578" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13579" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2902" class="Function Operator">_∙_</a><a id="13582" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="13649" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13650" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#13650" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13652" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#13652" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13654" </pre>
Horizontal concatination satisfies an additional "2-dimensional" unit law (on
both the left and right) induced by the unit laws on the boundary 1-paths.

### Unit laws for whiskering

</pre>
### The whiskering operations allow us to commute higher identifications

There are two natural ways to commute higher identifications: using whiskering
on the left versus using whiskering on the right. These two ways "undo" each
other.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="15523" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="15530" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#15530" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="15534" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15535" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#15535" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="15537" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15539" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="15544" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15546" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15547" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#15547" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15549" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15551" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="15554" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#15535" class="Bound">l</a><a id="15555" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15557" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15558" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#15558" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15560" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#15560" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="15562" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#15562" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="15564" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15566" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#15547" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15567" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="15571" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="15580" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#15580" class="Function">path-swap-nat-identification-left-whisk</a> <a id="15620" class="Symbol">:</a>

### Definition of horizontal inverse

2-paths have an induced inverse operation from the operation on boundary 1-paths

<pre class="Agda"><a id="16773" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="16780" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16780" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="16784" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16785" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16785" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="16787" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16789" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="16794" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16796" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16797" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16797" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16799" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16801" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="16804" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16785" class="Bound">l</a><a id="16805" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16807" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16808" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16808" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16810" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16810" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="16812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16814" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16797" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16815" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16817" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16818" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16818" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16820" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16820" class="Bound">p&#39;</a> <a id="16823" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16825" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16808" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16827" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="16829" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16810" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16830" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="16834" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="16843" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16843" class="Function">horizontal-inv-Id²</a> <a id="16862" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16864" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16818" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16866" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="16868" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16820" class="Bound">p&#39;</a> <a id="16871" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16873" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16874" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3206" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="16878" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16818" class="Bound">p</a><a id="16879" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16881" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="16883" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16884" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3206" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="16888" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16820" class="Bound">p&#39;</a><a id="16890" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="16894" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#16843" class="Function">horizontal-inv-Id²</a> <a id="16913" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16915" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="16918" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3206" class="Function">inv</a>
</pre>
This operation satisfies a left and right idenity induced by the inverse laws on
1-paths

### Action on 2-paths of functors

Functions have an induced action on 2-paths

Since this is define in terms of `ap`, it comes with the standard coherences. It
also has induced cohereces.

Inverse law.

      <a id="20413" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20415" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#6634" class="Function">nat-htpy</a> <a id="20424" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20425" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#2304" class="Function">ap-inv</a> <a id="20432" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#20109" class="Bound">f</a><a id="20433" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20435" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#20121" class="Bound">α</a><a id="20436" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20439" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2902" class="Function Operator">∙</a>

## Properties of 3-paths

3-paths are identifications of 2-paths. In symbols, a type of 3-paths is a type
of the form `α ＝ β` where `α β : p ＝ q` and `p q : x ＝ y`.

### Concatination in a type of 3-paths

Like with 2-paths, 3-paths have the standard operations on equalties, plus the
operations induced by the operations on 1-paths. But 3-paths also have
operations induced by those on 2-paths. Thus there are three ways to concatenate
in triple identity types. We name the three concatenations of triple identity
types x-, y-, and z-concatenation, after the standard names for the three axis
in 3-dimensional space.

The x-concatenation operation corresponds the standard concatination of
equalities.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="x-concat-Id³"></a><a id="22275" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22275" class="Function">x-concat-Id³</a> <a id="22288" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="22292" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22293" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22293" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="22295" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22297" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="22302" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22304" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22305" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22305" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22307" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22309" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="22312" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22293" class="Bound">l</a><a id="22313" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22315" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22316" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22316" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22318" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22318" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="22320" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22322" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22305" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22323" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22325" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22326" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22316" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22334" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22336" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22318" class="Bound">y</a><a id="22337" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22339" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22340" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22340" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="22342" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22342" class="Bound">β</a> <a id="22344" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22344" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="22346" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22348" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22326" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="22350" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22352" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22328" class="Bound">q</a><a id="22353" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22355" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="22359" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22340" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="22361" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22363" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22342" class="Bound">β</a> <a id="22365" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22367" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22342" class="Bound">β</a> <a id="22369" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22371" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22344" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="22373" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22375" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22340" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="22377" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22379" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22344" class="Bound">γ</a>
<a id="22381" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22275" class="Function">x-concat-Id³</a> <a id="22394" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22394" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="22396" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22396" class="Bound">τ</a> <a id="22398" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22400" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#7365" class="Function">vertical-concat-Id²</a> <a id="22420" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22394" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="22422" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22396" class="Bound">τ</a>
</pre>
The y-concatenation operation corresponds the operation induced by the
concatination on 1-paths.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="y-concat-Id³"></a><a id="22535" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22535" class="Function">y-concat-Id³</a> <a id="22548" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="22552" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22553" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22553" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="22555" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22557" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="22562" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22564" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22565" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22565" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22567" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22569" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="22572" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22553" class="Bound">l</a><a id="22573" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22575" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22576" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22576" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22578" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22578" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="22580" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22582" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22565" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22583" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22585" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22586" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22586" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="22588" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22588" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="22590" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22590" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="22592" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22594" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22576" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22596" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22598" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22578" class="Bound">y</a><a id="22599" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22601" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22602" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22602" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="22604" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22604" class="Bound">β</a> <a id="22606" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22608" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22586" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="22610" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22612" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22588" class="Bound">q</a><a id="22613" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="22617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22618" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22618" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="22620" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22620" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="22622" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22624" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22588" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="22626" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22628" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22590" class="Bound">r</a><a id="22629" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22633" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22602" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="22635" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22637" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22604" class="Bound">β</a> <a id="22639" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22641" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22618" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="22643" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22645" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22620" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="22647" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22649" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22650" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22602" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="22652" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2902" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="22654" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22618" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="22655" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22657" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1953" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="22659" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22660" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22604" class="Bound">β</a> <a id="22662" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2902" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="22664" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22620" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="22665" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="22667" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22535" class="Function">y-concat-Id³</a> <a id="22680" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22682" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#7495" class="Function">horizontal-concat-Id²</a>
</pre>
The z-concatenation operation corresponds the concatination induced by the
horizontal concatination on 2-paths.

    <a id="25709" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25711" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22535" class="Function">y-concat-Id³</a> <a id="25724" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25725" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22830" class="Function">z-concat-Id³</a> <a id="25738" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#25529" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="25740" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#25553" class="Bound">υ</a><a id="25741" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25743" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25744" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22830" class="Function">z-concat-Id³</a> <a id="25757" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#25541" class="Bound">τ</a> <a id="25759" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#25565" class="Bound">ϕ</a><a id="25760" class="Symbol">)))</a>
<a id="25764" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#25370" class="Function">interchange-y-z-concat-Id³</a> <a id="25791" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="25796" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="25801" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="25806" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1922" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="25811" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25813" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3206" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="25817" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3545" class="Function">right-unit</a>
</pre>
## Properties of 4-paths

The pattern for concatenation of 1, 2, and 3-paths continues. There are four
ways to concatenate in quadruple identity types. We name the three non-standard
concatenations in quadruple identity types `i`-, `j`-, and `k`-concatenation,
after the standard names for the quaternions `i`, `j`, and `k`.

### Concatenation of four paths

#### The standard concatination

<pre class="Agda"><a id="concat-Id⁴"></a><a id="26233" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#26233" class="Function">concat-Id⁴</a> <a id="26244" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="27275" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27067" class="Function">k-concat-Id⁴</a> <a id="27288" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27288" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="27290" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27290" class="Bound">τ</a> <a id="27292" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27294" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-binary-functions.html#855" class="Function">ap-binary</a> <a id="27304" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="27307" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27307" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="27309" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27309" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="27311" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27313" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#22830" class="Function">z-concat-Id³</a> <a id="27326" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27307" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="27328" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27309" class="Bound">n</a><a id="27329" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27331" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27288" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="27333" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27290" class="Bound">τ</a>
</pre>

              <a id="28796" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28798" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28800" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#3349" class="Function">assoc</a> <a id="28806" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#28209" class="Bound">p0̂00</a> <a id="28812" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#28239" class="Bound">p100̂</a> <a id="28818" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#28257" class="Bound">p10̂1</a><a id="28823" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28825" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2902" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
                <a id="28843" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28845" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="28847" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="28850" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28851" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2962" class="Function">concat</a> <a id="28858" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#28209" class="Bound">p0̂00</a> <a id="28864" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#27439" class="Bound">x111</a><a id="28868" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28870" href="foundation.path-algebra.html#28308" class="Bound">p10̂0̂</a><a id="28876" class="Symbol">)))))))</a>
